Ajit Vadakayil</a></cite><span class=\"icon user blog-author\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;data:image/png; background-repeat: no-repeat; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px -4px 6px; width: 18px;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"https://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2017/12/blockchain-bitcoin-big-brother-will.html?showComment=1513185259860#c4671100578196233665\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888;\">December 13, 2017 at 10:44 PM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_175MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nPhysicists in China and the US have built a 10-qubit superconducting quantum processor that could be scaled up to tackle problems not solvable by classical computers.<br />\n<br />\nQubits are the building blocks of quantum computing, capable of superposition \u2013 being in two states at the same time, rather than the computer bits of today, which are either a 1 or a 0 at any given moment.<br />\n<br />\nEntanglement is where quantum states can't be described independently, but only in relation to the others, making for a more solid system. The team used a measurement technique called quantum tomography to prove that they had indeed entangled their qubits<br />\n<br />\nThe phenomenon of entanglement in quantum physics, which has been observed in many experiments, implies that objects that are far removed in space (even across billions of miles) remain connected even though there is no mediating agency.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2011/01/quantum-entanglement-video-capt-ajit.html</span><br />\n<br />\nVedic philosophy tells us about the existence of another type of particle called the atma, the soul, the self, having different properties from those of ordinary particles.This is not unusual in physics, as is the case with antimatter particles.<br />\n<br />\nThe atma does not come into or out of existence, it is always present. It does not decay or degrade, it maintains its individuality always, it\u2019s infinitesimally small and it\u2019s not composed of more elementary particles. It\u2019s unchangeable, which along with the individuality property implies that it does not unite with other particles to create more complex structures, nor does it merge with others.<br />\n<br />\nThe atma does not interact directly with matter, but given that the atma is the source of consciousness and the life force in a living entity, any entity displaying them reveals the presence of an atma in it\u2014whether human, animal, plant, etc.<br />\n<br />\nVedanta wrote 7000 years ago-- The living entities are not made up of atmas; rather, they are these particles and are animating the material bodies that encase them. To find its value, it is calculated how much work it produces in a unit time.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nCONTINUED TO 3</div>\n<span class=\"comment-actions secondary-text\" id=\"bc_0_173MN\" kind=\"m\"><span class=\"item-control blog-admin pid-1783552029\" style=\"display: inline;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-replies\" id=\"bc_0_173BR\" style=\"margin-left: 36px; margin-top: 1em;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-replybox-single\" id=\"bc_0_173B_box\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; margin-top: 5px;\">\n</div>\n</li>\n<li class=\"comment\" id=\"bc_0_174B\" kind=\"b\" style=\"border-bottom: 0px; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0.25em 0px 0px;\"><div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"float: left; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c466643263114631994\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_174M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_174MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nCONTINUED FROM 2--<br />\n<br />\nMathematically, the rate of change in momentum i.e. the increment in work in unit time is proportional to the force in action. Also, this change is in the direction of the force. Suppose that the mass of an object is \u2018m\u2019 and in time interval \u2018t\u2019, the velocity of the object changes from \u2018u\u2019 to \u2018v\u2019 due to the force acting on it.<br />\n<br />\nThen, Initial momentum = m*u<br />\nFinal momentum = m*v<br />\nChange in momentum = m(v*u)<br />\nTherefore, the rate of change of momentum = m(v*u)/t<br />\nt = m*a (from Kanada\u2019s first law)<br />\n<br />\nFrom Kandas second law, force is proportional to the rate of change of momentum<br />\nOr, p = k*m*a (where k is a constant)<br />\nIf m=1 and a=1, then<br />\n1 = k*1*1 or k = 1<br />\nOr, p = m*a<br />\n<br />\nTherefore, unit force is the one that produces unit acceleration in an object of unit mass. The VS then goes to say that force is a result of work and is not a physical quantity which is superior to Newtons law that measures it as a physical quantity.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2011/01/isaac-newton-calculus-thief-capt-ajit.html</span><br />\n<br />\nThe sutras on energy:<br />\n<br />\nVaiseshika defines energy as being a radiant thing(i.e. energy is radiation) and energy is related totemperature and motion of a particle.<br />\n<br />\nVedic Indians understood the process of refraction and absorbtion of energy by \u201cmaterial obstructions\u201d and they understood heat, electricity and magnetism to be forms of energy. It is already understood by the elemental theory that light is also an energy and is composed of discreet units.<br />\n<br />\nThis was of course was not understood in modern times till Max Plank and Einstein in the 20th cetury devised quantum theory after the study of black body radiation and the photoelectric effect.<br />\n<br />\nCapt ajit vadakayil<br />\n..</div>\n</div>\n</li>\n</span></ol>\n<span id=\"bc_0_175b+seedBBVAD\" kind=\"d\">\n</span></div>\n</div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\nFibonacci was the first to introduce the Hindu-Arabic number system into Europe- the system we now use today- based on ten digits with its decimal point and a symbol for zero: 1 2 3 4 5 6 7 8 9. and 0</span></span></div>\n</div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 24px; margin: 0in;\">\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<br /></div>\n</div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 24px; margin: 0in;\">\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\"></span>A&nbsp;<b>golden rectangle</b>&nbsp;is a rectangle whose side lengths are in the&nbsp;<b>golden ratio</b>, 1: 1.618. whose reciprocal is 0.618033989 . . . . . so that we have 1/G = 1 + G.</span></div>\n</div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 24px; margin: 0in;\">\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n</div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ZQZhI9KexIo/TWZQ8X2lGbI/AAAAAAAADpw/XRcIUhVV9ww/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ZQZhI9KexIo/TWZQ8X2lGbI/AAAAAAAADpw/XRcIUhVV9ww/s1600/images+%25286%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 24px; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;\">\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 17px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"></span></span></div>\n</div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">The distance from the lower corners of the 2x1 rectangle to the top and bottom vertices of the Sri Yantra is PHI = (1/2)(diagonal of rectangle + 1) = (1/2)(sqrt(5) + 1). &nbsp;&nbsp;</span>Since PHI^2 = PHI + 1, the radius of the circle is sqrt(PHI^2 - 1^2) = sqrt ((PHI + 1) - 1) = sqrt(PHI). &nbsp;Let D be the distance between the base lines of the two largest triangles. Then the highest and lowest base lines are at distance D above and below the base lines of the two largest triangles. &nbsp;&nbsp;Everthing else is constructed symmetrically from those basic elements.</span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; margin-left: 3.75pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 3.75pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Gravity pushes--it does NOT pull, as told by Newton of apple bump on head fame.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 3.75pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 3.75pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In case light has to go through the body, then this body must be rotated out of this dimension, which we will not talk about in this post.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 3.75pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 3.75pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Light does not bend under an externally applied electric or magnetic field because the photon has no electric charge.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">But gravity bends light , as seen during the solar eclipse, where the intense gravitational field acts like a lens , diverting the starlight towards us.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 3.75pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\">\n<i><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><b><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></b></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-7Vji39ui71o/TV-WWF00oEI/AAAAAAAADiA/gBqmjNwhFOc/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-left: 3.75pt; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; text-align: justify;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The gravity of planets is static in comparison to light. For one to influence the other, resonance (matching in frequencies) must happen.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , serif;\">As soon as you modulate or vibrate gravity, light bends like a straw under its influence.&nbsp;This the&nbsp;closer you reach resonant frequency, the less intense the gravitational field needs to be.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Immerse a charged spherical object in a magnetic field </span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">. If you plot the gravity vector,at right angles to both electric and magnetic fields, it can be rotated &nbsp;around the object like a vortex.&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></i></b></span></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><b><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></i></b></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; It enters the field and gets side swiped, by the gravity vectors, sending it around the object.</span></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">As per laws of conservation of momentum, such a photon must swing back around the field, exactly, by the same amount it was deflected. This wont happen unless the photon exits from the field, the opposite side from where it entered.</span></span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Q= Charge</span></span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; It polymerises at temperatures &gt;30 deg C.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Synthetic rubber is a white milky emulsion of carboxylated Styrene-Butadeine Copolymer or hydrocarbon polymer . Wetting is being carried out light steam which should be cool prior loading.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Ships in Latex trade have special latex impellers. Japanese Kosaka pumps have a special latex box. Other ships need to blanked off at the impeller end. Bellmouth should be removed<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>and stainless steel blank with teflon gasket installed to seal pump bottom.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Upper opening of pump casing should be sealed with rubber and silicon and threaded hole for flushing to be plugged. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">You will need ladder telescopic aluminium ladders to access any spot inside the tank if cargo dries on tank sides and overhead after discharge.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Steam coils should be filled with fresh water as usual.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Diffusers, if installed to be removed from tank and stored for voyage. Drop lines should be blinded or plugged securely with wooden plugs.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Hi level alarm and floats should be removed from tank for the voyage. Sounding pipes<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>and vent lines should be plugged / corked with wooden plugs or scupper plugs of appropriate size. If latex gets into line then this will coagulate and it is easier to renew the line, than trying to remove the solidified latex.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Shippers sometimes insist that the coating failure spots should be painted with hot paraffin wax. The wax will have to be melted and painted over the rust spots with hand brushes. It dries up almost immediately. It is better that the whole tank is<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>sprayed with hot paraffin wax.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Sometimes the shipper may insist on formaldehyde fumigating epoxy tanks. Stainless steel does not require fumigation.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>This will be done by shore personnel.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Vessel should be supplied with 4-5 drums of Aqueous Ammonia ( Ammonium hydroxide ) to form seal and stop coagulation<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The coefficient of expansion is negligible. Since the latex will coagulate in the void space between the tank overhead and level of the liquid , the tanks should be always full loaded up into tank dome. To avoid air pockets it is better that the trim is even keel during loading.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">The cargo is dropped into the ships tank by a hose supplied by the Charterer. The outlet of the dropline must be submerged into the cargo throughout the loading to prevent foaming.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Upon completion of loading the aqueous ammonia should be poured<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>on top of latex into the tank dome<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>to form seal and prevent coagulation. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Since the latex coagulates, any heat adjacent must be avoided. Heat or dryness turns the latex into rubber.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Since vent lines will be plugged, ullage caps or vapour locks can <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>be cracked open daily for pressure release<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Vessel will be provided with portable hydraulic screw Framo pump on rent basis with hydraulic pressure and return hoses, cargo hoses and associated equipment, designed specially for latex.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Ship\u2019s hydraulic system will be used, therefore suitable coupling should be on board<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>to connect rented pump to ship\u2019s hydraulic lines. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Sufficient quantity of fresh water should be on board for pre washing cleaning the tanks .<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Prepare portable pump hired from shore, lower down into the tank through aft butterworth hatch.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Open tank lid, there will be solid layer on top of cargo . Remove to at open drum. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Start discharging. Portable pump should be fully submerged into the latex throughout the discharge to prevent clogging by floating scum.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Fresh water should be recirculated through the screw pump cofferdam seal during the discharge. If water flow stops or gets milky the discharging should be stopped and pump opened and cleaned of latex.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Prior to completion of discharge two men will need to enter tank to position pump in aft end for stripping while squeezing the tank top. All necessary precautions to be taken for entry into the tank with unsafe atmosphere .Ammonia can irritate the eyes.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Keep tank wet with ammonia spray during dischg. This way the coagulated rubber on bulkheads can be minimised. As soon a squeezing is over the surveyor must give tank dry certificate. Quickly give a FW cycle with one machine in all ports and leave the water at the bottom of tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><u><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">NEVER EVER</span></u></b><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\"> let the discharged tank become dry as Latex will polymerise. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">After sailing, outside 12 mile /25 metre zone, pump<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>out fresh water using portable eductor or Wilden<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>M15 pump. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Make tank gas free.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Put into tank the hose and wash ladder, heating coils u-bolts, pump with sea water<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Remove coagulated latex from the tank top .<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Using ladder peel out<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>rubber skin from the tank overhead, bulkheads and collect all latex from<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>heating coils.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Unseal cargo pump, remove blind flanges from drop lines, sounding pipe and vent line. Recirculate<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>pure chlorinated solvent ( Perchlorethylene ) for 3 hours. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">This solvent can be reused for 2 tanks provided a drum is added to each next tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Ensure that a cone A filter is installed on pump stack elbow to prevent butterworth machines clogging.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Butterworth with ambient sea water with graco injection of 0.5 % teepol .<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Flush with fresh water.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Re install Install level gauge float and Hi and Hi-Hi alarms floats.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Make sure the PV plugs are removed and no latex clogs vent lines.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">Note: <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">If the shippers want to use the ships manifold pipelines <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">Immediately after loading fill the manifold lines with fresh water.</b> If no ammonia is available then steam the tank for 15 min prior loading. During voyage steam the tank 10 min daily to keep the ullage space moist. During dischg steam via butterworth ports for 10 minutes every one hour . Prewash the tank immediately to shore after the tank dry cert is issued. Use can use toluene to wipe out latex if you do not have a chlorinated solvent.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-97beA2RXY8E/TV6we3P1YKI/AAAAAAAADgQ/ZaLE63nZ9LU/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-97beA2RXY8E/TV6we3P1YKI/AAAAAAAADgQ/ZaLE63nZ9LU/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 YEARS IN COMMAND )<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;\">..<o:p></o:p></span></div></div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt.
